### Creating New England

country_event = { # Player America gets a choice to swap to New England
	id = newengland.1
	immediate = { hidden_effect = { USA_emergency_recruitment_fix = yes } }
	title = newengland.1.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_Riots

	desc = {
		text = newengland.1.d.usa
		trigger = { tag = USA }
	}
	desc = {
		text = newengland.1.d.csa
		trigger = { tag = CSA }
	}
	desc = {
		text = newengland.1.d.psa
		trigger = { tag = PSA }
	}
	desc = {
		text = newengland.1.d.tex
		trigger = { tag = TEX }
	}

	trigger = { is_ai = no }

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # We will deal with this later
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.1 option newengland.1.a"
		name = newengland.1.a
	}

	option = { # Switch to New England
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.1 option newengland.1.b"
		name = newengland.1.b
		NEE = { change_tag_from = ROOT }
	}
}

country_event = { # ACW nation informed that Canada has seized New England
	id = newengland.2
	title = newengland.2.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_Riots

	desc = {
		text = newengland.2.d
		trigger = { country_exists = CSA }
	}
	desc = {
		text = newengland.2.d.nocsa
		trigger = { NOT = { country_exists = CSA } }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	major = yes
	show_major = {
		is_american_tag = yes
	}

	option = { # We will deal with this later
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.2 option newengland.2.a"
		name = newengland.2.a
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = FROM modifier = occupied_new_england }
	}
}

country_event = { # Canada doesn't occupy New England
	id = newengland.3
	title = newengland.3.t
	desc = newengland.3.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_Riots

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		country_exists = CSA
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.3 option newengland.3.a"
		name = newengland.3.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_new_england_units
		NEE_move_generals = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			create_USA_garrison_template = yes
			932 = {
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"Massachusetts Coastal Defense Force\" division_template = \"Defense Force\" start_experience_factor = 0.6"
					allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
					prioritize_location = 6732 #Boston
					owner = ROOT
					id = 1776
				}
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"Massachusetts National Guard\" division_template = \"Defense Force\" start_experience_factor = 0.6"
					allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
					prioritize_location = 6732 #Boston
					owner = ROOT
					id = 1776
				}
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"North-Eastern Department Reserve Force\" division_template = \"Defense Force\" start_experience_factor = 0.2"
					allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
					prioritize_location = 6732 #Boston
					owner = ROOT
					id = 1776
				}
			}
			933 = {
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"Vermont National Guard\" division_template = \"Defense Force\" start_experience_factor = 0.2"
					allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
					prioritize_location = 4445 #Montpelier
					owner = ROOT
					id = 1776
				}
			}
			932 = {
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"Rhode Island National Guard\" division_template = \"Defense Force\" start_experience_factor = 0.2"
					allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
					prioritize_location = 9832 #Providence
					owner = ROOT
					id = 1776
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Canada Debates Question of New England
	id = newengland.5
	title = newengland.5.t
	desc = newengland.5.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_spain_civil_war_soldiers

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.5 option newengland.5.a"
		name = newengland.5.a #Set up the provisional government
		ai_chance = {
			base = 75
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = CAN_acw_new_england option = CAN_ACW_NEW_ENGLAND_NOT_FORM }
			}
		}
		USA_spawn_new_england = yes
		NEE = {
			NEE_Starting_Great_Depression_Effect = yes
		}
		log = "KR_Event_Logging;NEE SPAWNED;[GetDateText]"
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.5 option newengland.5.b"
		name = newengland.5.b #Set up the provisional government (play as New England)
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		USA_spawn_new_england = yes
		NEE = {
			NEE_Starting_Great_Depression_Effect = yes
			change_tag_from = ROOT
		}
		log = "KR_Event_Logging;NEE SPAWNED;[GetDateText]"
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.5 option newengland.5.c"
		name = newengland.5.c #Continue with the military occupation
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_government = market_liberal
					has_government = social_liberal
					has_government = social_democrat
				}
				NOT = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = CAN_acw_new_england option = CAN_ACW_NEW_ENGLAND_NOT_FORM }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				has_government = paternal_autocrat
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = CAN_acw_new_england option = CAN_ACW_NEW_ENGLAND_FORM }
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = { is_core_of = NEE }
			if = {
				limit = { is_claimed_by = CAN }
				remove_claim_by = CAN
			}
			add_compliance = -25
		}
		add_war_support = -0.05
		set_country_flag = CAN_no_puppet_new_england
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = {
				CAN_yankee_rebellion = 0
			}
			country_event = { id = newengland.80 days = 25 random_days = 10 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_dlc_lar = yes }
				CAN = {
					create_operative_leader = {
						name = "Virginia Hall"
						GFX = GFX_portrait_kr_virginia_hall
						traits = { operative_demolition_expert }
						bypass_recruitment = no
						available_to_spy_master = yes
						female = yes
						nationalities = { CAN NEE USA CSA TEX PSA }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Independent New England
	id = newengland.6
	title = newengland.6.t
	desc = newengland.6.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_spain_civil_war_soldiers

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.6 option newengland.6.a"
		name = newengland.6.a
		add_political_power = 10
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = newengland.216 days = 90 }
			country_event = { id = newengland.54 days = 200 random_days = 100 }
			country_event = { id = newengland.64 days = 1100 } #This should probably get moved to the USA history file later so a more concrete date may be set.
			country_event = { id = newengland.59 days = 600 }
			country_event = { id = newengland.68 days = 60 random_days = 15 }
			country_event = { id = newengland.151 days = 400 random_days = 45 }
			country_event = { id = newengland.153 days = 245 random_days = 30 }
			country_event = { id = newengland.159 days = 353 }
			### Firing the flavour events
			NEE_Flavour_Events = yes
		}
	}
}

### Independence ###

country_event = { # New England requests home rule
	id = newengland.12
	title = newengland.12.t
	desc = newengland.12.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NEE = {
			is_subject_of = CAN
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.12 option newengland.12.a"
		name = newengland.12.a #give them home rule
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = var:NEE.NEE_legitimacy
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 250
				NEE = {
					has_country_flag = NEE_more_likely_independent
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.75
				NEE = {
					has_country_flag = less_likely_independence
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		effect_tooltip = {
			set_autonomy = {
				target = NEE
				autonomy_state = autonomy_free
			}
		}
		NEE = {
			clr_country_flag = NEE_more_likely_independent
			country_event = { id = newengland.13 days = 3 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.12 option newengland.12.b"
		name = newengland.12.b #refuse
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					NEE = { has_cosmetic_tag = america }
					strength_ratio = { tag = NEE ratio < 1.0 }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_authoritarian_government = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_government = social_liberal
					has_government = social_democrat
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_authoritarian_government = no
				check_variable = { NEE.NEE_legitimacy > 80 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				has_authoritarian_government = no
				check_variable = { NEE.NEE_legitimacy > 90 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_authoritarian_government = no
				check_variable = { NEE.NEE_legitimacy = 100 }
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 50
		NEE = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = CAN
				modifier = KR_outraged
			}
			country_event = { id = newengland.14 days = 3 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # New England granted home rule
	id = newengland.13
	title = newengland.13.t
	desc = newengland.13.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy3

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		is_subject_of = CAN
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.13 option newengland.13.a"
		name = newengland.13.a
		add_political_power = 50
		overlord = {
			set_autonomy = {
				target = NEE
				autonomy_state = autonomy_free
			}
		}
		NEE_Change_Legitimacy = yes
	}
}

country_event = { # New England refused home rule
	id = newengland.14
	title = newengland.14.t
	desc = newengland.14.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		is_subject_of = CAN
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.14 option newengland.14.a"
		name = newengland.14.a
		set_country_flag = NEE_refused_home_rule
		add_political_power = -50
		set_temp_variable = { NEE_legitimacy_change = -10 }
		NEE_Change_Legitimacy = yes
	}
}

country_event = { # Declaration of Independence
	id = newengland.15
	title = newengland.15.t
	desc = newengland.15.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.15 option newengland.15.a"
		name = newengland.15.a #We're fine with it
		ai_chance = { base = 75 }
		add_political_power = -100
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.15 option newengland.15.b"
		name = newengland.15.b #How dare they!
		trigger = {
			is_subject = no
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_elected_government = yes
					NOT = { is_faction_leader = yes }
					strength_ratio = {
						tag = NEE
						ratio < 1.0
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_war_support = 0.10
		add_stability = -0.05
		create_wargoal = {
			type = annex_everything
			target = FROM
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Remington Rand 1
	id = newengland.33

	desc = newengland.33.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

country_event = { # New England Hurricane
	id = newengland.40
	title = newengland.40.t
	desc = newengland.40.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NEE_hurricane

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	major = yes

	show_major = {
		OR = {
			controls_state = 357
			controls_state = 358
			controls_state = 359
			controls_state = 796
			controls_state = 930
			controls_state = 931
			controls_state = 932
			controls_state = 933
			controls_state = 934
			controls_state = 935
		}
	}

							}
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {

country_event = { # Creation of the Railroad
	id = newengland.50
	title = newengland.50.t
	desc = newengland.50.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # We can only do so much!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.50 option newengland.50.a"
		name = newengland.50.a
		add_political_power = 30
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { #CSA Refugees
				limit = {
					country_exists = CSA
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = NEE_ugr_csa_times
					value = 0
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = NEE_ugr_csa_manpower
					value = 2984
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = NEE_ugr_csa_guns
					value = 236
				}
				country_event = { id = newengland.51 days = 14 random_days = 7 } #Erie lake
				country_event = { id = newengland.55 days = 60 random_days = 7 } #Monthly intake refugees
			}
			if = { #TEX Refugees
				limit = {
					country_exists = TEX
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = NEE_ugr_tex_times
					value = 0
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = NEE_ugr_tex_manpower
					value = 2680
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = NEE_ugr_tex_guns
					value = 169
				}
				country_event = { id = newengland.56 days = 60 random_days = 7 } #Monthly intake refugees
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Refugees flood in from the Great Lakes (Underground Railroad)
	id = newengland.51
	title = newengland.51.t
	desc = newengland.51.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NEE_great_migration

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		country_exists = CSA
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = CSA
		}
		has_socialist_government = no
	}

	option = { # Send covert agents to assist the process
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.51 option newengland.51.a"
		name = newengland.51.a
		ai_chance = { base = 95 }
		add_political_power = -20
		add_manpower = 9874
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		random_list = {
			66 = {
				country_event = { id = newengland.52 days = 14 random_days = 7 }
			}
			34 = {
				country_event = { id = newengland.53 days = 8 random_days = 6 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Welcome to New England!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.51 option newengland.51.b"
		name = newengland.51.b
		ai_chance = { base = 5 }
		add_manpower = 9874
	}
}

country_event = { # Successful Smuggling action in the Great Lakes Region (Underground Railroad)
	id = newengland.52
	title = newengland.52.t
	desc = newengland.52.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NEE_great_migration

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		country_exists = CSA
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = CSA
		}
		has_socialist_government = no
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			multiply_variable = {
				var = NEE_ugr_csa_manpower
				value = 1.1
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				var = NEE_ugr_csa_guns
				value = 1.1
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # The Resistance grows Stronger!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.52 option newengland.52.a"
		name = newengland.52.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = NEE_ugr_csa_10p_increase
		add_manpower = 13789
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = infantry_equipment_1
			amount = 756
			producer = CSA
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = artillery_equipment_1
			amount = 23
			producer = CSA
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		random_list = {
			66 = {
				country_event = { id = newengland.52 days = 25 random_days = 7 }
			}
			34 = {
				country_event = { id = newengland.53 days = 8 random_days = 6 }
			}
		}
	}
}

### Rebellion Events ###
country_event = { # The Yankee Rebellion
	id = newengland.80
	title = newengland.80.t
	desc = newengland.80.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_soldiers_running
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = CAN
		is_subject = no
		OR = {
			357 = { is_owned_by = CAN } #Maine
			796 = { is_owned_by = CAN } #Albany
			930 = { is_owned_by = CAN } #Buffalo
			931 = { is_owned_by = CAN } #Connecticut
			932 = { is_owned_by = CAN } #Massachusetts
			933 = { is_owned_by = CAN } #Vermont
			934 = { is_owned_by = CAN } #New Hampshire
			935 = { is_owned_by = CAN } #Rhode Island
		}
		controls_all_owned_states = yes
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = CAN_no_puppet_new_england
			has_country_flag = { flag = CAN_seized_new_england days > 90 }
		}
		OR = {
			has_completed_focus = CAN_new_england_question
			NOT = { focus_progress = { focus = CAN_new_england_question progress > 0 } }
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = CAN_yankee_rebellion
			country_exists = NEE
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = {
				CAN_yankee_rebellion = 0
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.80 option newengland.80.a"
		name = newengland.80.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 75
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = CAN_acw_new_england option = CAN_ACW_NEW_ENGLAND_FORM }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_government = market_liberal
					has_government = social_liberal
					has_government = social_democrat
				}
				NOT = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = CAN_acw_new_england option = CAN_ACW_NEW_ENGLAND_NOT_FORM }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_government = paternal_autocrat
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = CAN_yankee_rebellion
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = { is_core_of = NEE }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = CAN_nee_resistance }
			add_to_variable = { var = ROOT.CAN_yankee_rebellion value = 1 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_resistance = no }
				start_resistance = yes
			}
			add_resistance = 25
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = {
						NOT = { has_country_flag = CAN_no_puppet_new_england }
					}
				}
				add_compliance = -25
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				CAN = { CAN_setup_NEE_suppression_decisions = yes }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = CAN_no_puppet_new_england }
			}
			set_country_flag = CAN_no_puppet_new_england
			add_stability = -0.05
			add_war_support = -0.05
			if = {
				limit = { has_dlc_lar = yes }
				CAN = {
					create_operative_leader = {
						name = "Virginia Hall"
						GFX = GFX_portrait_kr_virginia_hall
						traits = { operative_demolition_expert }
						bypass_recruitment = no
						available_to_spy_master = yes
						female = yes
						nationalities = { CAN NEE USA CSA TEX PSA }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_stability = -0.01
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.80 option newengland.80.b"
		name = newengland.80.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = CAN_no_puppet_new_england
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = CAN_acw_new_england option = CAN_ACW_NEW_ENGLAND_NOT_FORM }
			}
		}
		USA_spawn_new_england = yes
		NEE = {
			NEE_Starting_Great_Depression_Effect = yes
			#Popularities shifted to account for the rebellion
			hidden_effect = {
				set_popularities = {
					totalist = 0
					radical_socialist = 4
					syndicalist = 9
					social_democrat = 5
					social_liberal = 21
					market_liberal = 28
					social_conservative = 7
					authoritarian_democrat = 21
					paternal_autocrat = 2
					national_populist = 3
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		# Patrol battle
		add_manpower = -4
		CSA = { add_manpower = -13 }
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = infantry_equipment
			amount = 60
			producer = CSA
		}
		# Reduce guns
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = infantry_equipment
			amount = -250
			producer = NEE
		}
		# flag for less resistance
		set_country_flag = NEE_prepared_for_infil
	}

	option = { # Surely this is false information
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.87 option newengland.87.b"
		name = newengland.87.b
		# Patrol battle
		add_manpower = -4
		CSA = { add_manpower = -13 }
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = infantry_equipment
			amount = 60
			producer = CSA
		}
	}
}

	id = newengland.88
	title = newengland.88.t
	desc = {
		text = newengland.88.d.prepared
		trigger = {
			tag = NEE
			has_country_flag = NEE_prepared_for_infil
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = newengland.88.d.lax
		trigger = {
			tag = NEE
			NOT = { has_country_flag = NEE_prepared_for_infil }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = newengland.88.d.csa
		trigger = {
			tag = CSA
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_Riots
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			# Add resistance
			930 = {
				set_state_flag = has_resistance_forced_for_nee
				force_enable_resistance = NEE
				start_resistance = yes
				set_compliance = 30
				set_resistance = 0
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NEE = {
						has_country_flag = NEE_prepared_for_infil
					}
				}
				930 = {
					add_resistance = 30
					set_garrison_strength = 1
				}
			}
			else = {
				930 = {
					add_resistance = 60
					set_garrison_strength = 0.6
				}
			}
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # (NEE) - Secure the region!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.88 option newengland.88.a"
		name = newengland.88.a
		trigger = {
			tag = NEE
		}
		add_war_support = -0.01
	}

	option = { # (CSA) - This should teach them!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.88 option newengland.88.b"
		name = newengland.88.b
		trigger = {
			tag = CSA
		}
		add_war_support = 0.01
	}
}

### Rejoining the ACW Winner ###
country_event = { # New England receives request
	id = newengland.90
	title = newengland.90.t

	desc = {
		text = newengland.90.d.forced
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { NEE_legitimacy < NEE_threshold }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = newengland.90.d.choice
		trigger = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { NEE_legitimacy < NEE_threshold } }
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		FROM = {
			save_event_target_as = requester
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					has_elected_government = yes
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = NEE_threshold
				value = 40
			}
			else = {
				set_variable = {
					var = NEE_threshold
					value = 20
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.90 option newengland.90.a"
		name = newengland.90.a #It seems we have no choice...
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { NEE_legitimacy < NEE_threshold }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = CAN
				CAN = {
					is_subject = no
					NOT = { is_in_faction_with = FROM }
				}
			}
			CAN = {
				country_event = newengland.91
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = no
				}
				FROM = {
					change_tag_from = NEE
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				country_event = { id = newengland.93 hours = 8 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.90 option newengland.90.b"
		name = newengland.90.b #We should reunite
		trigger = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { NEE_legitimacy < NEE_threshold } }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 70
			modifier = {
				add = -45
				FROM = { has_socialist_government = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -15
				FROM = { has_socialist_government = yes }
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				check_variable = { NEE_legitimacy > 60 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				check_variable = { NEE_legitimacy > 80 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = CAN
				CAN = {
					is_subject = no
				}
			}
			CAN = {
				country_event = newengland.91
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = no
				}
				FROM = {
					change_tag_from = NEE
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				country_event = { id = newengland.93 hours = 8 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.90 option newengland.90.c"
		name = newengland.90.c #Refuse
		trigger = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { NEE_legitimacy < NEE_threshold } }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = { has_elected_government = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_in_faction_with = FROM
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 45
				FROM = { has_socialist_government = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 15
				FROM = { has_socialist_government = yes }
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
		}
		add_war_support = 0.10
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_political_power = 100
		set_country_flag = CAN_refused_rejoin_usa
		FROM = {
			set_country_flag = CAN_refused_new_england
			country_event = { id = newengland.99 hours = 8 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # New England has folded
	id = newengland.98
	title = newengland.98.t
	desc = newengland.98.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		country_exists = NEE
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = event_target:requester
			has_war_with = NEE
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.98 option newengland.98.a"
		name = newengland.98.a
		set_country_flag = CAN_yankee_rebellion
		annex_country = {
			target = NEE
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = { is_new_england = yes }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = CAN_nee_resistance }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			CAN = { CAN_setup_NEE_suppression_decisions = yes }
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_mainland_america = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_claimed_by = NEE
					}
					remove_claim_by = NEE
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = NEE
					}
					remove_core_of = NEE
				}
			}
		}
		event_target:requester = {
			set_country_flag = CAN_refused_new_england
			country_event = { id = newengland.99 days = 3 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # New England refused to join
	id = newengland.99
	title = newengland.99.t

	desc = {
		text = newengland.99.d.exists
		trigger = {
			country_exists = NEE
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = newengland.99.d.notexists
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				country_exists = NEE
			}
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			country_exists = NEE
			CAN = {
				any_owned_state = {
					region = 186
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = NEE
				}
				NEE = {
					save_event_target_as = war_country
				}
			}
			else = {
				CAN = {
					save_event_target_as = war_country
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
					is_new_england = yes
				}
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.99 option newengland.99.a"
		name = newengland.99.a #Then it's war!
		trigger = {
			can_declare_war_on = event_target:war_country
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_elected_government = no
			}
		}
		create_wargoal = {
			target = event_target:war_country
			type = annex_everything
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.99 option newengland.99.b"
		name = newengland.99.b #We'll deal with this later
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = { default_attack_AI_trigger_FROM = no }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_elected_government = yes
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -100
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = event_target:war_country
			modifier = KR_outraged
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # New England has joined anyhow
	id = newengland.100
	title = newengland.100.t
	desc = newengland.100.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = event_target:requester
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.100 option newengland.100.a"
		name = newengland.100.a #New England is ours!
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				country_exists = GBR
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = event_target:requester
					ratio < 1.0
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = event_target:requester
					ratio < 1.5
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = event_target:requester
					ratio > 2.0
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_elected_government = yes
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_new_england = yes
				NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
			}
			add_claim_by = ROOT
		}
		add_war_support = 0.10
		add_stability = -0.10
		declare_war_on = {
			target = event_target:requester
			type = annex_everything
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.100 option newengland.100.b"
		name = newengland.100.b #Let them have it
		ai_chance = { base = 90 }
		add_political_power = -100
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_claimed_by = ROOT
				is_new_england = yes
			}
			remove_claim_by = ROOT
		}
	}
}

### Great Depression ###

country_event = { # Hidden Event to slowly reduce the Great Depression National Spirit
	id = newengland.101
	title = KR.hidden.t
	desc = KR.hidden.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_spain_civil_war_soldiers #Maybe change this to something more accurate

	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.101 option KR.hidden.a"
		name = KR.hidden.a #Great
		ai_chance = { base = 95 }
		# If at war, reduce effects faster
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war = yes
				if = {
					limit = {
						any_enemy_country = {
							is_neighbor_of = NEE
						}
					}
					enemies_strength_ratio > 0.6
				}
				else = {
					enemies_strength_ratio > 1
				}
				any_enemy_country = {
					ic_ratio = {
						tag = ROOT
						ratio > 1
					}
				}
			}
			NEE_Reduce_Great_Depression_big = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = NEE_GD_build_speed_var
						value = 0
					}
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NEE_Great_Depression }
			}
			else = { country_event = { id = newengland.101 days = NEE_GD_timer_var } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = NEE_Mil_Dono_1
					has_idea = NEE_Mil_Dono_2
					has_idea = NEE_Mil_Dono_3
				}
			}
			NEE_Reduce_Great_Depression_regular = yes
			subtract_from_variable = { NEE_GD_timer_var = 3 }
			clamp_variable = { var = NEE_GD_timer_var min = 5 max = 110 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = NEE_Mil_Dono_2
				}
				subtract_from_variable = { NEE_GD_timer_var = 7 }
				clamp_variable = { var = NEE_GD_timer_var min = 5 max = 110 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = NEE_Mil_Dono_3
				}
				NEE_Reduce_Great_Depression_regular = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = NEE_GD_build_speed_var
						value = 0
					}
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NEE_Great_Depression }
			}
			else = { country_event = { id = newengland.101 days = NEE_GD_timer_var } }
		}
		# If at peace, reduce effects slowly
		else = {
			NEE_Reduce_Great_Depression_regular = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = NEE_GD_build_speed_var
						value = 0
					}
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NEE_Great_Depression }
			}
			else = { country_event = { id = newengland.101 days = NEE_GD_timer_var } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { USA = { has_completed_focus = USA_gwbill_fails } }
			add_to_variable = { NEE_GWFaill_helper_var = 10 }
		}
	}

	option = { #HELPER for GWBill Failing
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.101 option KR.hidden.a"
		name = KR.hidden.a #Great
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				USA = { has_completed_focus = USA_gwbill_fails }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = NEE.NEE_GWFaill_helper_var
			}
		}
		set_variable = { NEE_GWFaill_helper_var = 0 }
		# If at war, reduce effects faster
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war = yes
				if = {
					limit = {
						any_enemy_country = {
							is_neighbor_of = NEE
						}
					}
					enemies_strength_ratio > 0.6
				}
				else = {
					enemies_strength_ratio > 1
				}
				any_enemy_country = {
					ic_ratio = {
						tag = ROOT
						ratio > 1
					}
				}
			}
			NEE_Reduce_Great_Depression_big = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = NEE_GD_build_speed_var
						value = 0
					}
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NEE_Great_Depression }
			}
			else = { country_event = { id = newengland.101 days = NEE_GD_timer_var } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = NEE_Mil_Dono_1
					has_idea = NEE_Mil_Dono_2
					has_idea = NEE_Mil_Dono_3
				}
			}
			NEE_Reduce_Great_Depression_medium = yes
			subtract_from_variable = { NEE_GD_timer_var = 3 }
			clamp_variable = { var = NEE_GD_timer_var min = 5 max = 110 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = NEE_Mil_Dono_2
				}
				subtract_from_variable = { NEE_GD_timer_var = 7 }
				clamp_variable = { var = NEE_GD_timer_var min = 5 max = 110 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = NEE_Mil_Dono_3
				}
				NEE_Reduce_Great_Depression_medium = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = NEE_GD_build_speed_var
						value = 0
					}
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NEE_Great_Depression }
			}
			else = { country_event = { id = newengland.101 days = NEE_GD_timer_var } }
		}
		# If at peace, reduce effects slowly
		else = {
			NEE_Reduce_Great_Depression_medium = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = NEE_GD_build_speed_var
						value = 0
					}
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NEE_Great_Depression }
			}
			else = { country_event = { id = newengland.101 days = NEE_GD_timer_var } }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Fires of War - Removes Great Depression upon entrance into civil war
	id = newengland.102
	title = newengland.102.t
	desc = newengland.102.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_soldiers_running

	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = fires_of_war_fired
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.102 option newengland.102.a"
		name = newengland.102.a #Rally to the flag
		# Add flag
		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = fires_of_war_fired }
		# Make the timer of the Great Depression rapidly decrease
		subtract_from_variable = { NEE_GD_timer_var = 20 }
		clamp_variable = { var = NEE_GD_timer_var min = 5 max = 110 }
		# Up a mobilization level
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_idea = tot_economic_mobilisation
					has_idea = war_economy
				}
			}
			increase_mobilisation = yes
		}
		# Reduce stability while increasing war support
		add_stability = -0.1
		add_war_support = 0.1
	}
}

country_event = { # Prepare to enter war
	id = newengland.104
	title = newengland.104.t
	desc = newengland.104.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_soldiers_running

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.104 option newengland.104.a"
		name = newengland.104.a
		# Unlock Southern Fire
		# Check for PSA surrender in the independent path
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_subject = no
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ENT }
				CAN = {
					has_authoritarian_government = yes
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = CAN_supports_USA
						has_country_flag = CAN_supports_TEX
						has_country_flag = CAN_supports_noone
					}
				}
				PSA = {
					exists = yes
					surrender_progress > 0.05
				}
			}
			country_event = newengland.134
		}
	}
}

### Convincing CAN to back NEE in the 2ACW ###

# In the event that no one is backed - Begin to push for NEE as the Entente's best choice for winning the 2ACW
# If CAN backed another faction, they will decline NEE's request if the backed faction is winning (more powerful than the others combined)
# If CAN backed a faction that is currently losing, they are more likely to support

country_event = { # Reassess American Commitment
	id = newengland.123
	title = newengland.123.t
	desc = {
		text = newengland.123.d.noone
		trigger = {
			CAN = { has_country_flag = CAN_supports_noone }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = newengland.123.d.TEX
		trigger = {
			CAN = { has_country_flag = CAN_supports_TEX }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = newengland.123.d.PSA
		trigger = {
			CAN = { has_country_flag = CAN_supports_PSA }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = newengland.123.d.USA
		trigger = {
			CAN = { has_country_flag = CAN_supports_USA }
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_commons2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.123 option newengland.123.a"
		name = newengland.123.a # Decline NEE's terms
		trigger = {
			CAN = { has_country_flag = CAN_supports_noone }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 15
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				CSA = { num_of_controlled_states > 20 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				check_variable = { NEE.NEE_legitimacy > 65 }
			}
		}
		NEE = {
			set_temp_variable = { NEE_legitimacy_change = -5 }
			effect_tooltip = { NEE_Change_Legitimacy = yes }
			country_event = newengland.133
			set_country_flag = NEE_denied_ENT_support_acw
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.123 option newengland.123.b"
		name = newengland.123.b # TEX is the better option
		trigger = {
			CAN = { has_country_flag = CAN_supports_TEX }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 15
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				TEX = { num_of_controlled_states > 20 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				check_variable = { NEE.NEE_legitimacy > 65 }
			}
		}
		NEE = {
			set_temp_variable = { NEE_legitimacy_change = -5 }
			effect_tooltip = { NEE_Change_Legitimacy = yes }
			country_event = newengland.133
			set_country_flag = NEE_denied_ENT_support_acw
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.123 option newengland.123.c"
		name = newengland.123.c # PSA is the better option
		trigger = {
			CAN = { has_country_flag = CAN_supports_PSA }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 15
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				PSA = { num_of_controlled_states > 20 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				check_variable = { NEE.NEE_legitimacy > 65 }
			}
		}
		NEE = {
			set_temp_variable = { NEE_legitimacy_change = -5 }
			effect_tooltip = { NEE_Change_Legitimacy = yes }
			country_event = newengland.133
			set_country_flag = NEE_denied_ENT_support_acw
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.123 option newengland.123.e"
		name = newengland.123.e # USA is the better option
		trigger = {
			CAN = { has_country_flag = CAN_supports_USA }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 15
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				USA = { num_of_controlled_states > 20 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				USA = {
					has_government = paternal_autocrat
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				check_variable = { NEE.NEE_legitimacy > 65 }
			}
		}
		NEE = {
			set_temp_variable = { NEE_legitimacy_change = -5 }
			effect_tooltip = { NEE_Change_Legitimacy = yes }
			country_event = newengland.133
			set_country_flag = NEE_denied_ENT_support_acw
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.123 option newengland.123.f"
		name = newengland.123.f # Agree to NEE's terms
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = NEE.NEE_legitimacy
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				NOT = { NEE = { has_idea = NEE_limited_recognation1 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				check_variable = { NEE.NEE_GD_consumer_goods_var < 15 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				NEE = { has_same_government_as_ROOT = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				NEE = {
					has_army_manpower = { size > 100000 }
				}
			}
			modifier = { #If the other tag is the Entente, CAN should decline this
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					is_in_faction_with = TEX
					is_in_faction_with = PSA
					is_in_faction_with = USA
				}
			}
			modifier = { #If fighting alongside another tag, don't bail on them
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_war_with = TEX
					has_war_with = PSA
					has_war_with = USA
				}
			}
		}
		NEE = {
			effect_tooltip = { NEE_Change_Legitimacy = yes }
			country_event = newengland.132
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_subject = no
					controls_all_owned_states = yes
					check_variable = { NEE_legitimacy > 49 }
					has_army_manpower = { size > 150000 }
					num_divisions > 20
					num_of_factories > 45
				}
				activate_decision = NEE_claim_usa_territory_harsh
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = ACW_support_usa }
				USA = { country_event = newengland.126 } #ACW Faction informed that the Entente is pulling out
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = ACW_support_psa }
				PSA = { country_event = newengland.126 } #ACW Faction informed that the Entente is pulling out
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = ACW_support_aus }
				TEX = { country_event = newengland.126 } #ACW Faction informed that the Entente is pulling out
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_in_faction_with = CAN }
				country_event = newengland.125 #Entente is informed of the two week pull out
			}
		}
	}
}

# If CAN declines the above, NEE gets a decision to consult with them agains when they have X legitimacy
# The more legitimacy NEE has, the more likely for CAN to agree to the subsequent event

				}
			}
			modifier = { #Don't support NEE if gamerule was set to only declare on CSA, or to never declare
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_acw_intervene
						option = CAN_ACW_INTERVENE_NO
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_acw_intervene
						option = CAN_ACW_INTERVENE_DECLARE_CSA
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = { #Don't support NEE if gamerule is set to support a specific side (unless they don't exist), or to support no one
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAN_acw_support
						option = CAN_ACW_SUPPORT_NONE
					}
					AND = {
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = CAN_acw_support
							option = CAN_ACW_SUPPORT_USA
						}
						USA = { exists = yes }
					}
					AND = {
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = CAN_acw_support
							option = CAN_ACW_SUPPORT_PSA
						}
						PSA = { exists = yes }
					}
					AND = {
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = CAN_acw_support
							option = CAN_ACW_SUPPORT_TEX
						}
						TEX = { exists = yes }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		NEE = {
			effect_tooltip = { NEE_Change_Legitimacy = yes }
			country_event = newengland.132
			clr_country_flag = NEE_denied_ENT_support_acw
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_subject = no
					controls_all_owned_states = yes
					check_variable = { NEE_legitimacy > 49 }
					has_army_manpower = { size > 150000 }
					num_divisions > 20
					num_of_factories > 45
				}
				activate_decision = NEE_claim_usa_territory_harsh
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = ACW_support_usa }
				USA = { country_event = newengland.126 } #ACW Faction informed that the Entente is pulling out
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = ACW_support_psa }
				PSA = { country_event = newengland.126 } #ACW Faction informed that the Entente is pulling out
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = ACW_support_aus }
				TEX = { country_event = newengland.126 } #ACW Faction informed that the Entente is pulling out
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_in_faction_with = CAN }
				country_event = newengland.125 #Entente is informed of the two week pull out
			}
		}
	}
}

# The Entente fully wades into the 2ACW backing NEE's claim to be the legitimate America

country_event = { # Pulling the Entente out of the backed faction
	id = newengland.127
	title = newengland.127.t
	desc = newengland.127.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_soldiers_watching

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.127 option newengland.127.a"
		name = newengland.127.a # Pull Entente Support Out
		# Clear CAN's support for other tags
		clr_country_flag = CAN_supports_noone
		clr_country_flag = CAN_supports_TEX
		clr_country_flag = CAN_supports_PSA
		clr_country_flag = CAN_supports_USA

		# Remove ACW support idea
		# General Entente Idea
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = ACW_support_usa }
			remove_ideas = ACW_support_usa
			recall_volunteers_from = USA
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = ACW_support_psa }
			remove_ideas = ACW_support_psa
			recall_volunteers_from = PSA
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = ACW_support_aus }
			remove_ideas = ACW_support_aus
			recall_volunteers_from = TEX
		}
		# NEE specific
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = NEE_support_usa }
			remove_ideas = NEE_support_usa
			recall_volunteers_from = USA
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = NEE_support_psa }
			remove_ideas = NEE_support_psa
			recall_volunteers_from = PSA
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = NEE_support_aus }
			remove_ideas = NEE_support_aus
			recall_volunteers_from = TEX
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = NEE }
			set_temp_variable = { NEE_legitimacy_change = 10 }
			NEE_Change_Legitimacy = yes
		}
	}
}

# CSA becomes aware of possible intervention
country_event = {
	id = newengland.128
	title = newengland.128.t
	desc = newengland.128.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_parliament1

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = CSA
		is_subject = no
		NEE = {
			is_subject = no
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = USA
				has_war_with = PSA
				has_war_with = TEX
				has_war_with = CSA
			}
			OR = {
				has_completed_focus = NEE_Reassess_American_Involvement
				focus_progress = {
					focus = NEE_Reassess_American_Involvement
					progress > 0.25
				}
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 3
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { NEE_strike_cost = 50 }
			NEE = {
				set_variable = { CSA_strikes = 0 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.128 option newengland.128.a"
		name = newengland.128.a
		set_country_flag = CSA_can_delay_new_england
		unlock_decision_tooltip = CSA_delay_new_england_intervention
	}
}

	id = newengland.139
	title = newengland.139.t
	desc = newengland.139.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_civil_war

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.139 option newengland.139.a"
		name = newengland.139.a #Liberty Rings Out
		trigger = {
			tag = NEE
		}
		set_country_flag = NEE_entered_the_civil_war
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = newengland.188 days = 36 } }
		if = {
			limit = {
				PSA = { has_war_with = CSA }
				NOT = { has_war_with = CSA }
			}
			add_to_war = { targeted_alliance = PSA enemy = CSA }
			hidden_effect = {
				CSA = {
					add_ai_strategy = {
						type = prepare_for_war
						id = NEE
						value = -100
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				PSA = { has_war_with = USA }
				NOT = { has_war_with = USA }
			}
			add_to_war = { targeted_alliance = PSA enemy = USA }
			hidden_effect = {
				USA = {
					add_ai_strategy = {
						type = prepare_for_war
						id = NEE
						value = -100
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				PSA = { has_war_with = TEX }
				NOT = { has_war_with = TEX }
			}
			add_to_war = { targeted_alliance = PSA enemy = TEX }
			hidden_effect = {
				TEX = {
					add_ai_strategy = {
						type = prepare_for_war
						id = NEE
						value = -100
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.139 option newengland.139.b"
		name = newengland.139.b #Yay!
		trigger = {
			tag = PSA
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.139 option newengland.139.c"
		name = newengland.139.c #We will crush them too!
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = NEE
				tag = PSA
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = newengland.175

	desc = {
		text = newengland.175.d.puppetger

			OR = {
				has_subject = GRU
				has_subject = RHI
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = newengland.175.d.notpuppetger
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_subject = GRU }
			NOT = { has_subject = RHI }
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_NEE_Bank

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_country_leader = { character = NEE_maurice_tobin }
			has_country_leader = { character = NEE_william_harriman }
		}
		OR = {
			781 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GRU }
			781 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = RHI }
		}
		OR = {
			51 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GRU }
			51 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = RHI }
		}
	}

	option = { # Turn America into a Pariah
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.175 option newengland.175.a"
		name = newengland.175.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_subject = GRU
				has_subject = RHI
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		add_political_power = -400
		781 = {
			remove_building = {
				type = arms_factory
				level = var:781.building_level@arms_factory
			}
			remove_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = var:781.building_level@industrial_complex
			}
		}
		51 = {
			remove_building = {
				type = arms_factory
				level = var:51.building_level@arms_factory
			}
			remove_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = var:51.building_level@industrial_complex
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Use more than 2 braincells
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.175 option newengland.175.b"
		name = newengland.175.b
	}
}

### Election Events ###

# Use this code to set the most recent elections and frequency #

# meta_effect = {
# 	text = {
# 		set_politics = {
# 			ruling_party = market_liberal
# 			last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
# 			election_frequency = 48
# 			elections_allowed = yes
# 		}
# 	}

country_event = { #Provisional President
	id = newengland.200
	title = newengland.200.t
	desc = newengland.200.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress #Potentially grab a pic of the MA statehouse to use in the Election events

	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = PSA_Leader }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = NEE_had_provisional_election }
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			end_coalition = yes
			country_event = { id = newengland.210 days = 16 }
			country_event = { id = newengland.160 days = 700 }
			country_event = { id = newengland.1550 days = 500 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.200 option newengland.200.a"
		name = newengland.200.a #The Republican Candidate - Barrows
		ai_chance = { base = 35 }
		set_country_flag = NEE_had_provisional_election
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = market_liberal
			last_election = "1936.11.16"
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		promote_character = NEE_lewis_barrows
		hidden_effect = {
			NEE_lewis_barrows = {
				add_trait = { trait = NEE_provisional_president ideology = market_liberal_subtype }
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = NEE_provisional_president_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = newengland.152 days = 167 }
			country_event = { id = newengland.156 days = 234 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.200 option newengland.200.b"
		name = newengland.200.b #The Compromise Cabinet - Martin Jr.
		ai_chance = { base = 15 }
		set_country_flag = NEE_had_provisional_election
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = market_liberal
			last_election = "1936.11.16"
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		promote_character = NEE_joseph_martin_jr
		hidden_effect = {
			NEE_joseph_martin_jr = {
				add_trait = { trait = NEE_provisional_president ideology = market_liberal_subtype }
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = NEE_provisional_president_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		custom_effect_tooltip = NEE_unity_cabinet_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { NEE.coalition_stability = 0.5 }
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_liberal }
			add_to_coalition = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.200 option newengland.200.c"
		name = newengland.200.c #The Democratic Candidate - Walsh
		ai_chance = { base = 50 }
		set_country_flag = NEE_had_provisional_election
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_liberal
			last_election = "1936.11.16"
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		promote_character = NEE_david_walsh
		hidden_effect = {
			NEE_david_walsh = {
				add_trait = { trait = NEE_provisional_president ideology = social_liberal_subtype }
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = NEE_provisional_president_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.05
		}

		# Fire next event

			country_event = { id = newengland.218 days = 13 }
		}
	}

	option = { #Restrict
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.217 option newengland.217.b"
		name = newengland.217.b
		# Add idea
		add_ideas = NEE_Fair_Labour_idea_2

country_event = { # Fair Labour 2 - Minimum Wage
	id = newengland.218
	title = newengland.218.t
	desc = newengland.218.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NEE_Child_Labor_Standard

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Enact
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.218 option newengland.218.a"
		name = newengland.218.a
		# Idea Swap
		if = { # Keep - Enact
			limit = {
				has_idea = NEE_Fair_Labour_idea_1
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = NEE_Fair_Labour_idea_1
				add_idea = NEE_Fair_Labour_idea_3
			}
		}
		else_if = { # Restrict - Enact
			limit = {
				has_idea = NEE_Fair_Labour_idea_2
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = NEE_Fair_Labour_idea_2
				add_idea = NEE_Fair_Labour_idea_5
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Reject this syndicalism!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.218 option newengland.218.b"
		name = newengland.218.b
		# Idea Swap
		if = { # Keep - Reject
			limit = {
				has_idea = NEE_Fair_Labour_idea_1
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = NEE_Fair_Labour_idea_1
				add_idea = NEE_Fair_Labour_idea_4
			}
		}
		else_if = {  # Restrict - Reject
			limit = {
				has_idea = NEE_Fair_Labour_idea_2
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = NEE_Fair_Labour_idea_2
				add_idea = NEE_Fair_Labour_idea_6
			}
		}
	}
}

### AALA Factory Events ###

country_event = { # [NEE] decide how many factories to send
	id = newengland.230
	title = newengland.230.t
	desc = newengland.230.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_factory_workers

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag
			has_war_with = TEX
			has_war_with = CSA
			has_war_with = USA
			has_war_with = PSA
		}
	}

	option = { # Send them 1 Factory
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.230 option newengland.230.a"
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { NEE.num_of_military_factories > 1 }
		}
		name = newengland.230.a
		# Give NEE a timed idea that removes [1] military factory for 90 days
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = NEE_Mil_Dono_1
			days = 90
		}
		army_experience = 5
		set_variable = { NEE_sent_mil = 1 }
		# Get the reverse variable as well
		set_variable = { NEE_sent_mil_removal = NEE_sent_mil }
		multiply_variable = { NEE_sent_mil_removal = -1 }
		# Add the offmap mil to the backed country and
		# Send an event to the backed faction that they are receiving [1] NEE factory for 90 days
		effect_tooltip = {
			NEE_factory_donation_tt_to_backed_faction_1 = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			NEE_apply_factory_donation_to_backed_faction = yes
		}
	}

	option = { # Send them 2 Factories
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.230 option newengland.230.b"
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { NEE.num_of_military_factories > 5 }
		}
		name = newengland.230.b
		# Give NEE a timed idea that removes [2] military factory for 90 days
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = NEE_Mil_Dono_2
			days = 90
		}
		army_experience = 10
		set_variable = { NEE_sent_mil = 2 }
		# Get the reverse variable as well
		set_variable = { NEE_sent_mil_removal = NEE_sent_mil }
		multiply_variable = { NEE_sent_mil_removal = -1 }
		# Add the offmap mils to the backed country and
		# Send an event to the backed faction that they are receiving [2] NEE factories for 90 days
		effect_tooltip = {
			NEE_factory_donation_tt_to_backed_faction_2 = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			NEE_apply_factory_donation_to_backed_faction = yes
		}
	}

	option = { # Send them 3 Factories
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.230 option newengland.230.c"
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { NEE.num_of_military_factories > 10 }
		}
		name = newengland.230.c
		# Give NEE a timed idea that removes [3] military factory for 90 days
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = NEE_Mil_Dono_3
			days = 90
		}
		army_experience = 15
		set_variable = { NEE_sent_mil = 3 }
		# Get the reverse variable as well
		set_variable = { NEE_sent_mil_removal = NEE_sent_mil }
		multiply_variable = { NEE_sent_mil_removal = -1 }
		# Add the offmap mils to the backed country and
		# Send an event to the backed faction that they are receiving [3] NEE factories for 90 days
		effect_tooltip = {
			NEE_factory_donation_tt_to_backed_faction_3 = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			NEE_apply_factory_donation_to_backed_faction = yes
		}
	}

	option = { # Don't send anything
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.230 option newengland.230.e"
		name = newengland.230.e
		# Give NEE another event in 90 days to determine how many factories to send
		hidden_effect = {
			NEE = {
				country_event = { id = newengland.230 days = 90 }
			}
		}
	}
}

	# 	has_global_flag = USA_PSA_existed

						is_character = USA_omar_nelson_bradley
						is_character = USA_leonard_townsend_gerow
						is_character = USA_edwin_forrest_harding

						is_character = USA_william_frederick_halsey_jr
						is_character = USA_raymond_ames_spruance
					}
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				every_character = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_character = USA_dwight_david_eisenhower
							is_character = USA_omar_nelson_bradley
							is_character = USA_leonard_townsend_gerow
							is_character = USA_edwin_forrest_harding
							is_character = USA_john_clifford_hodges_lee
							is_character = USA_frank_jack_fletcher

			}

	id = newengland.274
	title = newengland.274.t
	desc = newengland.274.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_strike

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.274 option newengland.274.a"
		name = newengland.274.a
		NEE_Reduce_Syndicalist_Terrorist = yes
		# Fill Garrison strength in CSA states
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = CSA
				has_resistance = yes
			}
			set_garrison_strength = 1.0
		}
		add_stability = -0.01
		add_war_support = -0.01
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = USA_longist_resistance4
			}
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = newengland.279 days = 65 random_days = 50 } }
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = newengland.280 days = 90 random_days = 50 } }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # NEE requests land + NAP from CAN (CAN Event)
	id = newengland.300
	title = newengland.300.t
	desc = newengland.300.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy3

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.300 option newengland.300.a"
		ai_chance = { base = 90 }
		name = newengland.300.a # Accept the deal
		# Friendship Modifier
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = NEE
			modifier = KR_approves_of_govt
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = NEE
			modifier = KR_approves_of_govt
		}
		# CAN and the Entente return American territory
		NEE_Returning_American_Land_effect_tt = yes
		# Mutual NAP to secure the Northern Border
		diplomatic_relation = {
			country = NEE
			relation = non_aggression_pact
			active = yes
		}
		NEE = {
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = CAN
				relation = non_aggression_pact
				active = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.300 option newengland.300.b"
		trigger = {
			ENT = { #Entente at war with the Internationale
				has_war_with = INT
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				CAN = {
					has_authoritarian_government = yes
				}
			}
		}
		name = newengland.300.b
		add_political_power = -50
		effect_tooltip = {
			NEE = { add_political_power = 50 }
		}
		# One way NAP from CAN
		diplomatic_relation = {
			country = NEE
			relation = non_aggression_pact
			active = yes
		}
		# Use this flag in the on_action for CAN vs ENG peace deal
		set_country_flag = nee_loaned_american_territory
		hidden_effect = {
			NEE = { #Allow NEE to accept the promise or decline
				country_event = newengland.304
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #No. I don't think I will
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.300 option newengland.300.c"
		trigger = {
			CAN = {
				is_ai = no
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		name = newengland.300.c
		add_political_power = -100
		set_country_flag = nee_can_rejects_nee_request
		NEE = { #Inform NEE that CAN is keeping the land
			country_event = newengland.304
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Partial or Total Denial of terms from the Buffalo Conference
	id = newengland.304
	title = newengland.304.t
	desc = {
		text = newengland.304.d.return # Canada returns the territory they control
		trigger = {
			CAN = {
				has_country_flag = nee_returns_american_territory
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = newengland.304.d.partial # Canada requests to keep the territory for the duration of the war
		trigger = {
			CAN = {
				has_country_flag = nee_loaned_american_territory
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = newengland.304.d.total # Total Rejection of return
		trigger = {
			CAN = {
				has_country_flag = nee_can_rejects_nee_request
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy3

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.304 option newengland.304.a"
		name = newengland.304.a # Allow the temporary loan
		trigger = {
			CAN = {
				has_country_flag = nee_loaned_american_territory
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 40 }
		CAN = { clr_country_flag = nee_loaned_american_territory }
		add_political_power = 50
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.304 option newengland.304.b"
		name = newengland.304.b # This is unacceptable
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				CAN = {
					has_country_flag = nee_returns_american_territory
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 60
			modifier = {
				add = 140
				CAN = {
					has_country_flag = nee_can_rejects_nee_request
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				strength_ratio = { tag = CAN ratio < 1.0 }
			}
		}
		CAN = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = nee_loaned_american_territory
				}
				clr_country_flag = nee_loaned_american_territory
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = nee_can_rejects_nee_request
				}
				clr_country_flag = nee_can_rejects_nee_request
			}
		}
		CAN = { country_event = newengland.305 }
		add_war_support = 0.05
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.304 option newengland.304.c"
		name = newengland.304.c # Allow CAN to retain the territory
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
			NOT = {
				CAN = {
					has_country_flag = nee_returns_american_territory
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 25
				strength_ratio = { tag = CAN ratio > 2.0 }
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_political_power = -50
		CAN = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = nee_loaned_american_territory
				}
				clr_country_flag = nee_loaned_american_territory
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = nee_can_rejects_nee_request
				}
				clr_country_flag = nee_can_rejects_nee_request
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.304 option newengland.304.e"
		name = newengland.304.e # CAN returns the territory
		trigger = {
			CAN = {
				has_country_flag = nee_returns_american_territory
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		NEE_Returning_American_Land = yes
		add_stability = 0.05
		CAN = { clr_country_flag = nee_returns_american_territory }
	}
}

					has_government = paternal_autocrat
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				OR = {

	id = newengland.309
	title = newengland.309.t
	desc = newengland.309.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy3

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.309 option newengland.309.a"
		name = newengland.309.a # Offer them support if they reject terms
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 70
				MEX = {
					OR = {
						has_government = syndicalist
						has_government = radical_socialist
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				MEX = {
					has_government = totalist
				}
			}
			modifier = { #Add +25 if the ENT is gone
				add = 25
				NOT = {
					ENT = { exists = yes }
				}
			}
			modifier = { #Add +75 if GER is gone
				add = 75
				NOT = {
					GER = { exists = yes }
				}
			}
		}
		MEX = {
			set_country_flag = { flag = nee_int_supports_mex days = 30 value = 1 }
			country_event = newengland.310
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.309 option newengland.309.b"
		name = newengland.309.b # Inform them that we cannot support them
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				MEX = { #MEX base chances
					OR = {
						has_government = syndicalist
						has_government = radical_socialist
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						ENT = { exists = yes } #ENT still around
						GER = { exists = yes } #GER still standing
					}
				}
			}
		}

		MEX = {
			set_country_flag = { flag = nee_int_bails_on_mex days = 30 value = 1 }
			country_event = newengland.310
		}
	}
}

			MEX = {
				has_country_flag = nee_mex_denies_terms
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				strength_ratio = { tag = MEX ratio > 1.5 }
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -100
	}
}

country_event = { #NEE invites us into the OAS
	id = newengland.316
	title = newengland.316.t
	desc = newengland.316.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.316 option newengland.316.a"
		name = newengland.316.a # Join
		ai_chance = {
			base = 70
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				NEE = { has_government = social_liberal }
				OR = {
					has_government = social_liberal
					has_government = social_democrat
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				NEE = { has_government = market_liberal }
				OR = {
					has_government = market_liberal
					has_government = social_conservative
				}
			}
			modifier = { #CA countries are more likely to join if their neighbours are in the OAS. (Same with BRA URG and VEN)
				add = 20
				is_in_central_america = yes
				OR = {
					tag = BRA
					tag = URG
					tag = VEN
				}
				any_neighbor_country = {
					is_in_faction_with = NEE
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				tag = BRA
				has_government = social_conservative
			}
		}
		NEE = {
			set_country_flag = { flag = wishes_to_join_OAS value = 1 days = 15 }
			country_event = newengland.317
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.316 option newengland.316.b"
		name = newengland.316.b # Decline
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = { # SA countries are less likely to join if their neighbours are in the OAS
				add = 20
				is_in_south_america = yes
				NOT = {
					tag = BRA
					tag = URG
					tag = VEN
				}
				any_neighbor_country = {
					is_in_faction_with = NEE
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
				FROM = {
					is_in_central_america = yes
				}
				count_triggers = {
					amount = 1
					PAN = { is_in_faction_with = NEE }
					COS = { is_in_faction_with = NEE }
					GUA = { is_in_faction_with = NEE }
					ELS = { is_in_faction_with = NEE }
					HON = { is_in_faction_with = NEE }
					NIC = { is_in_faction_with = NEE }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
				FROM = {
					is_in_central_america = yes
				}
				count_triggers = {
					amount = 2
					PAN = { is_in_faction_with = NEE }
					COS = { is_in_faction_with = NEE }
					GUA = { is_in_faction_with = NEE }
					ELS = { is_in_faction_with = NEE }
					HON = { is_in_faction_with = NEE }
					NIC = { is_in_faction_with = NEE }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -10
				FROM = {
					is_in_central_america = yes
				}
				count_triggers = {
					amount = 4
					PAN = { is_in_faction_with = NEE }
					COS = { is_in_faction_with = NEE }
					GUA = { is_in_faction_with = NEE }
					ELS = { is_in_faction_with = NEE }
					HON = { is_in_faction_with = NEE }
					NIC = { is_in_faction_with = NEE }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NEE = { has_government = social_liberal }
				OR = {
					has_government = social_liberal
					has_government = social_democrat
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NEE = { has_government = market_liberal }
				OR = {
					has_government = market_liberal
					has_government = social_conservative
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = declined_to_join_OAS
		NEE = {
			country_event = newengland.317
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #FROM answers our invite to the OAS
	id = newengland.317
	title = newengland.317.t
	desc = {
		text = newengland.317.d1
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = wishes_to_join_OAS
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = newengland.317.d2
		trigger = {
			FROM = { has_country_flag = declined_to_join_OAS }
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.317 option newengland.317.a"
		name = newengland.317.a # Welcome!
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = wishes_to_join_OAS
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			add_to_faction = FROM
		}
		else = { #Backup redundancy - NEE should never lose leadership of the OAS
			faction_leader = {
				add_to_faction = FROM
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.317 option newengland.317.b"
		name = newengland.317.b # Aw Shucks
		trigger = {
			FROM = { has_country_flag = declined_to_join_OAS }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		add_political_power = -25
	}
}

country_event = { #NEE asks us to leave our faction
	id = newengland.318
	title = newengland.318.t
	desc = newengland.318.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.318 option newengland.318.a"
		name = newengland.318.a # Inform the faction head
		if = {
			limit = { is_subject = yes }
			overlord = { country_event = newengland.319 }
		}
		else = {
			faction_leader = { country_event = newengland.319 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #NEE requests we abandon FROM
	id = newengland.319
	title = newengland.319.t
	desc = newengland.319.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.319 option newengland.319.a"
		name = newengland.319.a # Drop them
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = { #If the American fleet is superior, reconsider our position abroad
				add = 3
				naval_strength_ratio = {
					tag = NEE
					ratio > 1
				}
			}
			modifier = { #If the American army is superior, reconsider our position abroad
				add = 1
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = NEE
					ratio > 1
				}
			}
			modifier = { #If the Americans have a direct border, this could be dicier
				add = 5
				FROM = {
					is_neighbor_of = NEE
				}
			}
			modifier = { #If the Americans have a faction border, this could be dicier
				add = 1
				FROM = {
					any_neighbor_country = {
						is_in_faction_with = NEE
					}
				}
			}
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				clear_all_relations = yes
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			# Inform target country that they are being dropped from the faction
			set_country_flag = { flag = dropped_faction_member value = 1 days = 15 }
			country_event = newengland.321
		}
		# Inform NEE that the target country is being dropped from the faction
		NEE = { country_event = newengland.320 }
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.319 option newengland.319.b"
		name = newengland.319.b # We support our friends
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				tag = INT
				GER = { exists = no }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				tag = GER
				INT = { exists = no }
				RUS = { exists = no }
			}
			modifier = {
				#check number of allied states in the western hemisphere
				set_temp_variable = { num = 0 }
				all_of_scopes = {
					array = THIS.faction_members
					if = {
						limit = {
							FROM = { is_in_central_america = yes }
							is_in_central_america = yes
						}
						add_to_temp_variable = { num = 2 }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { is_in_central_america = yes }
						add_to_temp_variable = { num = 1 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							FROM = { is_in_south_america = yes }
							is_in_south_america = yes
						}
						add_to_temp_variable = { num = 2 }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { is_in_south_america = yes }
						add_to_temp_variable = { num = 1 }
					}
				}
				add = num
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = NEE_OAS_declines_terms_tt
		FROM = {
			set_country_flag = nee_declined_to_leave_faction
		}
		NEE = { country_event = newengland.320 }
	}
}

# FROM.FROM in 320 refers to the country that NEE requested that they leave their European Faction
# FROM is the European Faction leader

country_event = { #NEE receives answer from European faction leader
	id = newengland.320
	title = {
		text = newengland.320.t1
		trigger = {
			FROM.FROM = {
				has_country_flag = dropped_faction_member
			}
		}
	}
	title = {
		text = newengland.320.t2
		trigger = {
			FROM.FROM = { has_country_flag = nee_declined_to_leave_faction }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = newengland.320.d1
		trigger = {
			FROM.FROM = {
				has_country_flag = dropped_faction_member
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = newengland.320.d2
		trigger = {
			FROM.FROM = { has_country_flag = nee_declined_to_leave_faction }
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.320 option newengland.320.a"
		name = newengland.320.a # Monroe upheld!
		trigger = {
			FROM.FROM = {
				has_country_flag = dropped_faction_member
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		add_political_power = 25
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = KR_approves_of_govt
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = KR_approves_of_govt
		}
		# Add 2nd level of tensions here
		FROM.FROM = {
			add_to_variable = {
				NEE_Tensions = 2
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.320 option newengland.320.b"
		name = newengland.320.b # Don't push the issue
		trigger = {
			FROM.FROM = {
				has_country_flag = nee_declined_to_leave_faction
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 15 }
		FROM = { # Add one tension to the faction leader
			add_to_variable = {
				NEE_Tensions = 1
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		# Decrease opinion against faction leader
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = KR_disapproves_of_govt
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = KR_disapproves_of_govt
		}
		# FROM.FROM can stay in the faction!
		FROM.FROM = { country_event = newengland.322 }
		# FROM.FROM can stay in the faction! - Faction Leader
		FROM = { country_event = newengland.322 }
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.320 option newengland.320.c"
		name = newengland.320.c # This cannot stand
		trigger = {
			FROM.FROM = {
				has_country_flag = nee_declined_to_leave_faction
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0 #AI should never do this at first
			modifier = {
				#check tension level with faction leader
				set_temp_variable = { num = FROM.NEE_Tensions }
				multiply_temp_variable = {
					num = 10
				}
				add = num
			}
			modifier = { #If the European army is superior, reconsider war
				factor = 0.25
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio > 1
				}
			}
			modifier = { #If the European fleet is superior, reconsider war
				factor = 0.25
				naval_strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio > 1
				}
			}
		}
		create_wargoal = {
			type = annex_everything
			target = FROM.FROM
		}
		# Faction informed about the war
		FROM.FROM = { country_event = newengland.323 }
		FROM = { country_event = newengland.323 }
	}
}

# Terms are as follows: CEN must dissolve into constituent states but are all welcome into the OAS

country_event = { #Dem CEN given terms
	id = newengland.327
	title = newengland.327.t
	desc = {
		text = newengland.327.d1
		trigger = {
			has_elected_government = yes
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = newengland.327.d2
		trigger = {
			has_authoritarian_government = yes
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.327 option newengland.327.a"
		name = newengland.327.a # We accept the terms
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 70
				has_elected_government = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				has_authoritarian_government = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				NEE = { has_government = social_liberal }
				OR = {
					has_government = social_liberal
					has_government = social_democrat
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				NEE = { has_government = market_liberal }
				OR = {
					has_government = market_liberal
					has_government = social_conservative
				}
			}
			modifier = { #CA countries are more likely to join if their neighbours are in the OAS. (Same with BRA URG and VEN)
				add = 20
				any_neighbor_country = {
					is_in_faction_with = NEE
				}
			}
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 316 }
				release = COS
			}
			release = GUA
			release = NIC
			release = HON
			release = ELS
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 316 }
				set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = COS }
				release_targeted_CENtag_no_puppet = yes
				COS = { set_politics = { ruling_party = social_conservative } }
				NEE = { add_to_faction = COS }
			}

			GUA_restore_missing_characters = yes
			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = GUA }
			release_targeted_CENtag_no_puppet = yes
			GUA = { set_politics = { ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat } }
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 311 }
				GUA = {
					transfer_state = 311
					add_state_claim = 311
				}
			}

			NIC_restore_missing_characters = yes
			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = NIC }
			release_targeted_CENtag_no_puppet = yes
			NIC = { set_politics = { ruling_party = social_liberal } }

			HON_restore_missing_characters = yes
			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = HON }
			release_targeted_CENtag_no_puppet = yes
			HON = { set_politics = { ruling_party = social_conservative } }

			ELS_restore_missing_characters = yes
			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = ELS }
			release_targeted_CENtag_no_puppet = yes
			ELS = { set_politics = { ruling_party = social_liberal } }
		}
		NEE = {
			add_to_faction = GUA
			add_to_faction = NIC
			add_to_faction = HON
			add_to_faction = ELS
			set_country_flag = { flag = accepts_terms value = 1 days = 15 }
			country_event = newengland.328
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.327 option newengland.327.b"
		name = newengland.327.b # We decline the terms
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				has_elected_government = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 70
				has_authoritarian_government = yes
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = KR_disapproves_of_govt
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = KR_disapproves_of_govt
		}
		set_country_flag = declined_to_join_OAS
		NEE = {
			country_event = newengland.328
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #American Investors making moves in [FROM.GetNameDef]
	id = newengland.329
	title = newengland.329.t
	desc = newengland.329.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.329 option newengland.329.a"
		name = newengland.329.a # Embrace them
		ai_chance = {
			base = 2
			modifier = {
				add = 4
				any_neighbor_country = {
					has_idea = NEE_Investments_idea
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				set_temp_variable = { num = 0 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { num = American_Investor_Influence }
				add = num
			}
		}
		# timed flag for description
		set_country_flag = { flag = allows_investors value = 1 days = 15 }
		# timed idea
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = NEE_Investments_idea
			days = 100
		}
		# add to variable counter
		add_to_variable = {
			American_Investor_Influence = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					American_Investor_Influence > 2
				}
			}
			country_event = newengland.331 # People want to go free
		}
		NEE = {
			country_event = newengland.330 # NEE told investors are allowed
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.329 option newengland.329.b"
		name = newengland.329.b # Throw them out
		ai_chance = { base = 4 }
		# add to variable counter
		add_to_variable = {
			American_Investor_Tension = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					American_Investor_Tension > 2
				}
			}
			country_event = newengland.331 # Investor Chaos
		}
		# timed flag for description
		set_country_flag = { flag = declines_investors value = 1 days = 15 }
		NEE = {
			country_event = newengland.330
		}
	}
}
