			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.2
				tag = IRE
				NEE = {
					NOT = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = nee_ito_tt
		hidden_effect = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITO_member_dynamic_modifier } }
		NEE = {
			country_event = newengland.352
			add_to_variable = { var_ITO_members = 0.01 }
			force_update_dynamic_modifier = yes
		}
		force_update_dynamic_modifier = yes
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.351 option newengland.351.b"
		name = newengland.351.b # No thanks, I'll be poor
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = NEE
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = does_not_want_to_join_ITO
		NEE = { country_event = newengland.352 }
	}
}

# NEE considers inviting Ireland
country_event = {
	id = newengland.354
	title = newengland.354.t
	desc = {
		text = newengland.354.d1
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				IRE = {
					controls_state = 119
				}
				GBR = {
					NOT = { has_cosmetic_tag = GBR_britain }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = newengland.354.d2
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				IRE = {
					NOT = {
						controls_state = 119
					}
					GBR = {
						has_cosmetic_tag = GBR_britain
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_dail_meeting

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Invite IRE
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.354 option newengland.354.a"
		name = newengland.354.a
		IRE = { country_event = { id = newengland.355 days = 4 } }
	}

	option = { #Let's avoid the IRE of the British :hehe:
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.354 option newengland.354.b"
		name = newengland.354.b
	}
}

# IRE receives invite to Entente
country_event = {
	id = newengland.355
	title = newengland.355.t
	desc = newengland.355.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_capitol_hill

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Join the Entente
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.355 option newengland.355.a"
		name = newengland.355.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				add = 35
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat
				controls_state = 119
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -50
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat
				NOT = { controls_state = 119 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				has_government = social_conservative
				controls_state = 119
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 0
				has_government = social_conservative
				NOT = { controls_state = 119 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				has_government = market_liberal
				controls_state = 119
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 35
				has_government = market_liberal
				NOT = { controls_state = 119 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 0
				has_government = social_liberal
				controls_state = 119
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -45
				has_government = social_liberal
				NOT = { controls_state = 119 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 0
				has_government = social_democrat
				controls_state = 119
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -45
				has_government = social_democrat
				NOT = { controls_state = 119 }
			}
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			NEE = { add_to_faction = IRE }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			NEE = {
				country_event = { id = newengland.356 days = 4 }
				set_country_flag = { flag = ire_joining_entente value = 1 days = 15 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Politely decline
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.355 option newengland.355.b"
		name = newengland.355.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				add = -35
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat
				controls_state = 119
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat
				NOT = { controls_state = 119 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -50
				has_government = social_conservative
				controls_state = 119
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				has_government = social_conservative
				NOT = { controls_state = 119 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -20
				has_government = market_liberal
				controls_state = 119
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -35
				has_government = market_liberal
				NOT = { controls_state = 119 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 0
				has_government = social_liberal
				controls_state = 119
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 45
				has_government = social_liberal
				NOT = { controls_state = 119 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 0
				has_government = social_democrat
				controls_state = 119
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 45
				has_government = social_democrat
				NOT = { controls_state = 119 }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			NEE = {
				country_event = { id = newengland.356 days = 4 }
				set_country_flag = { flag = ire_declines_entente value = 1 days = 15 }
			}
		}
	}
}

## SFA ##
country_event = { #Invited to SFA
	id = newengland.365
	title = newengland.365.t
	desc = newengland.365.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.365 option newengland.365.a"
		name = newengland.365.a # We will join
		ai_chance = {
			base = 3
			# Add modifier here to increase chances to join
			modifier = {
				add = THIS.NEE_Friendly
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = is_SFA_member
		add_to_tech_sharing_group = nee_research
		hidden_effect = {
			NEE = { country_event = newengland.366 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.365 option newengland.365.b"
		name = newengland.365.b # Not interested right now
		ai_chance = { base = 2 }
		set_country_flag = { flag = does_not_want_to_join_SFA_temp days = 150 value = 1 }
		add_to_variable = {
			NEE_Tensions = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					NEE_Tensions > 4
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = hostile_tag_to_NEE
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			NEE = { country_event = newengland.366 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.365 option newengland.365.c"
		name = newengland.365.c # Not interested ever
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		set_country_flag = does_not_want_to_join_SFA
		hidden_effect = {
			NEE = { country_event = newengland.366 }
		}
	}
}

# Influence
country_event = { #Americans offer investments to entice us to join SFA
	id = newengland.372
	title = newengland.372.t
	desc = newengland.372.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.372 option newengland.372.a"
		name = newengland.372.a # We will allow them entry
		ai_chance = {
			base = 7
			# Add modifier here to increase chances to join
			modifier = {
				add = 3
				has_elected_government = yes
			}
		}
		# Bribe
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = NEE_Investments_idea
			days = 180
		}
		# AI modifier
		add_to_variable = {
			NEE_Friendly = 2
		}
		set_country_flag = { flag = allowed_SFA_influence days = 15 value = 1 }
		hidden_effect = {
			NEE = { country_event = newengland.373 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.372 option newengland.372.b"
		name = newengland.372.b # Not interested right now
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			# Reduce the chances if target is authoritarian
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				has_authoritarian_government = yes
			}
			# Less likely if in faction with Japan
			modifier = {
				add = 3
				is_in_faction_with = JAP
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			NEE_Tensions = 2
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					NEE_Tensions > 4
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = hostile_tag_to_NEE
		}
		set_country_flag = { flag = does_not_want_SFA_influence_temp days = 150 value = 1 }
		hidden_effect = {
			NEE = { country_event = newengland.373 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.372 option newengland.372.c"
		name = newengland.372.c # Not interested ever
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		set_country_flag = does_not_want_SFA_influence
		hidden_effect = {
			NEE = { country_event = newengland.373 }
		}
	}
}

			is_in_faction = yes
			is_faction_leader = no
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = newengland.380.d.default
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_in_faction = no
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
		}
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_WIF_Palms

	}

	option = { #Tell the faction leader we wish to rejoin

		name = newengland.380.a

			base = 60
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_socialist_government = no
						event_target:america = { has_socialist_government = yes }
					}
					AND = {
						has_socialist_government = yes
						event_target:america = {
							has_socialist_government = no
							NOT = { has_government = social_democrat }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			is_in_faction = yes
			is_faction_leader = no
		}

	}

		}
		trigger = {
			is_in_faction = yes
			is_faction_leader = no

		}

	}

				is_in_faction = no

	}

		trigger = {

				is_in_faction = no
				is_faction_leader = yes

country_event = { #The Philippines rejoin America
	id = newengland.383
	title = newengland.383.t
	desc = newengland.383.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_WIF_Palms

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = FROM
			has_war_with = FROM.FROM #PHI's faction leader
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Excellent
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.383 option newengland.383.a"
		name = newengland.383.a
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_in_faction = yes }
				faction_leader = { save_event_target_as = former_faction_leader }
				leave_faction = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { is_faction_leader = yes }
				dismantle_faction = yes
			}
			separate_peace_all_wars = yes
		}
		FROM = { get_current_government_type = yes }
		set_autonomy = {
			target = FROM
			autonomy_state = kr_autonomous_puppet
			end_wars = no
		}
		FROM = {
			restore_previous_government_type = yes
			if = {
				limit = { has_elected_government = no }
				country_event = newengland.396
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = PHI_defied_faction_leader }
			event_target:former_faction_leader = { country_event = { id = newengland.385 days = 1 } }
		}
	}
}

		text = newengland.391.d.annexed_same_faction
		trigger = {
			owns_state = 327
			is_in_faction_with = FROM
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = newengland.391.d.annexed
		trigger = {
			owns_state = 327
			NOT = { is_in_faction_with = FROM }
		}
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_WIF_Palms

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_war_with = FROM }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Return the American lands
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.391 option newengland.391.a"
		name = newengland.391.a
		trigger = { is_in_faction_with = FROM }
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		effect_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = { PHI = { is_subject = yes } }
				var:PHI.overlord = {
					set_autonomy = {
						target = PHI
						autonomy_state = autonomy_free
					}
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = { is_american_pacific_islands = yes }
				transfer_state_to = FROM
			}
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = newengland.392 days = 2 } }
	}

	option = { #No, we shall keep it
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.391 option newengland.391.b"
		name = newengland.391.b
		trigger = { is_in_faction_with = FROM }
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		FROM = { country_event = { id = newengland.393 days = 2 } }
	}

	option = { #The Philippines aren't worth fighting over
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.391 option newengland.391.c"
		name = newengland.391.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = { is_in_faction_with = FROM }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				add = -80
				OR = {
					tag = JAP
					AND = {
						has_socialist_government = no
						FROM = { has_socialist_government = yes }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = { PHI = { is_subject = yes } }
				var:PHI.overlord = {
					set_autonomy = {
						target = PHI
						autonomy_state = autonomy_free
					}
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = { is_american_pacific_islands = yes }
				transfer_state_to = FROM
			}
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = newengland.392 days = 2 } }
	}

	option = { #The Philippines belong to us
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.391 option newengland.391.d"
		name = newengland.391.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = { is_in_faction_with = FROM }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				OR = {
					tag = JAP
					AND = {
						has_socialist_government = no
						FROM = { has_socialist_government = yes }
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					tag = JAP
					AND = {
						has_socialist_government = no
						FROM = { has_socialist_government = yes }
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				strength_ratio = { tag = FROM ratio < 1 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				strength_ratio = { tag = FROM ratio < 1.5 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				strength_ratio = { tag = FROM ratio > 2 }
			}
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = newengland.395 days = 2 } }
	}
}

# 410 - 1940 PSA led election

country_event = { # 1940 Presidential Election
	id = newengland.410
	title = newengland.410.t
	desc = {
		text = newengland.410.d.normal #No Socdems
		trigger = { PSA_can_elect_farmer_labor = no }
	}
	desc = {
		text = newengland.410.d.socdem #PSA allows Socdem if USA is dead
		trigger = { PSA_can_elect_farmer_labor = yes }
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_PSA_Olson_McNary

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = newengland.209 days = 3 } } # Reset the congress mechanic for 1940
	}

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			tag = PSA
			has_country_flag = PSA_Leader
		}
		NOT = { has_country_flag = NEE_had_1940_election }
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.410 option newengland.410.a"
		name = newengland.410.a #Democrat - Olson
		set_country_flag = NEE_had_1940_election
		ai_chance = {
			base = 75
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_country_leader = { character = PSA_hiram_johnson }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = PSA
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = PSA_path option = PSA_PATH_MARLIB }
					AND = {
						has_game_rule = { rule = PSA_path option = PSA_PATH_SOCDEM }
						NOT = { country_exists = USA }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = social_liberal
					last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
					election_frequency = 48
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
			}
			CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
		}
		promote_character = PSA_culbert_olson
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.05
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.410 option newengland.410.b"
		name = newengland.410.b #Republican - McNary
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = PSA
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = PSA_path option = PSA_PATH_SOCLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = PSA_path option = PSA_PATH_SOCDEM }
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = NEE_had_1940_election
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = market_liberal
					last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
					election_frequency = 48
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
			}
			CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
		}
		promote_character = PSA_charles_mcnary
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			popularity = 0.05
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.410 option newengland.410.c"
		name = newengland.410.c #Farmer Labor - Wallace
		trigger = { PSA_can_elect_farmer_labor = yes }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = PSA
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = PSA_path option = PSA_PATH_SOCLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = PSA_path option = PSA_PATH_MARLIB }
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = NEE_had_1940_election
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = social_democrat
					last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
					election_frequency = 48
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
			}
			CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
		}
		promote_character = PSA_henry_wallace
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ustates.179 days = 60 random_days = 660 }
		}
	}
}

# 411-413 - 1944 PSA led election
country_event = {
	id = newengland.411 #hidden event to fire the correct version of the election (donotlog)
	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			tag = PSA
			has_country_flag = PSA_Leader
		}
		has_country_flag = NEE_had_1940_election
		NOT = { has_country_flag = NEE_had_1944_election }
		has_democratic_government = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = newengland.209 days = 3 } } # Reset the congress mechanic
	}

	option = {
		set_country_flag = NEE_had_1944_election
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { character = PSA_culbert_olson }
			}
			country_event = newengland.412 #Olson vs Lee
		}
		else = {
			country_event = newengland.413 #Warren vs Downey
		}
	}
}

				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = PSA_path option = PSA_PATH_MARLIB }
					AND = {
						has_game_rule = { rule = PSA_path option = PSA_PATH_SOCDEM }
						NOT = { country_exists = USA }
					}

			promote_character = PSA_earl_warren
			promote_character = PSA_philip_la_follette
		}
	}

		}
	}

	option = {

		trigger = {

# 414-417 - 1948 PSA led election
country_event = {
	id = newengland.414 #hidden event to fire the correct version of the election (donotlog)
	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			tag = PSA
			has_country_flag = PSA_Leader
		}
		has_country_flag = NEE_had_1944_election
		NOT = { has_country_flag = NEE_had_1948_election }
		has_democratic_government = yes
	}

	option = {
		set_country_flag = NEE_had_1948_election
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { character = PSA_sheridan_downey }
			}
			country_event = newengland.415 #Warren vs Downey
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_leader = { character = PSA_culbert_olson }
					has_country_leader = { character = PSA_earl_warren }
				}
			}
			country_event = newengland.416 #Martin vs Warren
		}
		else = {
			country_event = newengland.417 #Martin vs Lee
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Warren vs Downey
	id = newengland.415
	title = newengland.415.t

	desc = {
		text = newengland.415.d.PSA
		trigger = { PSA_can_elect_farmer_labor = yes }
	}
	desc = {
		text = newengland.415.d.NEE
		trigger = { PSA_can_elect_farmer_labor = no }
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_PSA_Warren_Downey

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.415 option newengland.415.a"
		name = newengland.415.a #Democrat - Downey
		ai_chance = {
			base = 55
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = PSA
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = PSA_path option = PSA_PATH_MARLIB }
					AND = {
						has_game_rule = { rule = PSA_path option = PSA_PATH_SOCDEM }
						NOT = { country_exists = USA }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		USA_conservative_democrats_elected_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			promote_character = PSA_glen_taylor
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.415 option newengland.415.b"
		name = newengland.415.b #Republican - Warren
		ai_chance = {
			base = 45
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = PSA
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = PSA_path option = PSA_PATH_SOCLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = PSA_path option = PSA_PATH_SOCDEM }
				}
			}
		}
		USA_republicans_elected_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			promote_character = PSA_glen_taylor
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.415 option newengland.415.c"
		name = newengland.415.c #Farmer Labor - Taylor
		trigger = { PSA_can_elect_farmer_labor = yes }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 35
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = PSA
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = PSA_path option = PSA_PATH_SOCLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = PSA_path option = PSA_PATH_MARLIB }
				}
			}
		}
		promote_character = PSA_glen_taylor
		PSA_farmer_labor_elected_effect = yes
	}
}

			}
			country_event = newengland.419 #Martin vs Cain

				has_country_leader = { character = PSA_sheridan_downey }

			country_event = newengland.420 #Magnuson vs Cain
		}

		}

			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = PSA
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = PSA_path option = PSA_PATH_SOCLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = PSA_path option = PSA_PATH_MARLIB }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_leader = { character = PSA_glen_taylor ruling_only = no } } }
			promote_character = PSA_glen_taylor
		}
		PSA_farmer_labor_elected_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			promote_character = PSA_warren_magnuson
			promote_character = PSA_richard_nixon
		}
	}
}

### Using Legitimacy Events ###

country_event = {
	id = newengland.441
	title = newengland.441.t
	desc = newengland.441.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_alufactory

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Accept the contract
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.441 option newengland.441.a"
		name = newengland.441.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				add = NEE.NEE_legitimacy
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 30
		# Add negative idea for CAN
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = NEE_neg_infantry_contract_idea
			days = 90
		}
		# Event to NEE
		NEE = {
			set_country_flag = { flag = can_accepts_contract days = 15 value = 1 }
			country_event = newengland.442
		}
	}

	option = { #We cannot accept
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.441 option newengland.441.b"
		name = newengland.441.b
		ai_chance = { base = 20 }
		NEE = {
			set_country_flag = { flag = can_declines_contract days = 15 value = 1 }
			country_event = newengland.442
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = newengland.442
	title = {
		text = newengland.442.t.accept
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = can_accepts_contract
		}
	}
	title = {
		text = newengland.442.t.decline
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = can_declines_contract
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = newengland.442.d.accept
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = can_accepts_contract
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = newengland.442.d.decline
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = can_declines_contract
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy3

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # ENT accepted the contract
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.442 option newengland.442.a"
		name = newengland.442.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = can_accepts_contract
		}
		# Add postive idea for NEE
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = NEE_pos_infantry_contract_idea
			days = 90
		}
		# Loss of legitimacy
		set_temp_variable = { NEE_legitimacy_change = -15 }
		NEE_Change_Legitimacy = yes
	}

	option = { # ENT declined the contract
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.442 option newengland.442.b"
		name = newengland.442.b
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = can_declines_contract
		}
		# Refund
		add_political_power = 10
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = newengland.900
	title = KR.test.t
	desc = KR.test.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.900 option KR.test.a"
		name = KR.test.a
		add_ideas = NEE_civil_war_aftermath_idea
		add_ideas = USA_civil_war_depression_idea
		add_ideas = USA_longist_resistance1
		set_country_flag = NEE_has_longist_terrorists
		add_ideas = USA_socialist_resistance1
		set_country_flag = NEE_has_syndicalist_terrorists
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		add_ideas = civilian_economy
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = NEE_Reorganise_National_Guard
				has_idea = selective_training_act
			}
			add_ideas = special_forces_focus
		}
		add_stability = -0.25
		add_war_support = -0.6
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = PSA
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = newengland.400 days = 3 }
				PSA = { country_event = { id = newengland.400 days = 3 } }
			}
		}
	}
}

# 451 - PP (talks with Gov) -- 20%
# 452 - Stab (Speech to people) -- 30%
# 453 - WS (Address to military) -- 5%

# 455 - Bombers (Lancasters from Malton Ontario by Victory Aircraft) -- 8%
# 456 - Fighters (CAN fighter1s from Malton Ontario by National Steel Car) -- 12%
# 457 - offmap factory (After talks with C.D.Howe, site prepared in NEE for factory) -- 5% - more likely if Howe is minister in CAN
# 458 - temp prod. growth/output (Ambassador invites CAN industrialists to help improve NEE) -- 8%
# 459 - Legitimacy (Ambassador hosting big American-Canada friendship speech) -- 20% - early game
# 460 - MP support (Mounties offer support) -- 20% - post reconstruction

country_event = { #Hidden Looper event
	id = newengland.450
	title = KR.hidden.t
	desc = KR.hidden.d

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_idea_with_trait = NEE_ambassador_to_canada
	}

	option = { #PP Event
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.450 option KR.hidden.a"
		name = KR.hidden.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_country_flag = recently_had_PP
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				has_political_power < 0
			}
		}
		country_event = newengland.451
	}

	option = { #Stability Event
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.450 option KR.hidden.a"
		name = KR.hidden.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_country_flag = recently_had_stability
			}
		}
		country_event = newengland.452
	}

	option = { #War Support Event

			base = 5

					has_trait = NEE_ambassador_to_canada

	option = { #Trucks Event

			}
		}
		country_event = newengland.455
	}

	option = { #Fighter Event

			base = 12
			modifier = {

				has_country_flag = recently_had_fighters
			}
		}
		country_event = newengland.456
	}

	option = { #Offmap Factory Event

# 460 - MP support (Mounties offer support)
country_event = { # MP Support event
	id = newengland.460
	title = newengland.460.t
	desc = newengland.460.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_army1

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.460 option newengland.460.a"
		name = newengland.460.a
		NEE = {
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					has_resistance = yes
				}
				set_garrison_strength = 1
				add_resistance = -5
				add_compliance = 5
			}
		}
		add_manpower = 200
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = newengland.450 days = 80 random_days = 10 }
		}
	}
}

# 461 - Replace Winant
country_event = { # Replace Winant
	id = newengland.461
	title = newengland.461.t
	desc = {
		text = newengland.461.d.rep
		trigger = {
			has_government = market_liberal
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = newengland.461.d.dem
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_liberal
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy5

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.461 option newengland.461.a"
		name = newengland.461.a #Moffat's our man!
		trigger = {
			NEE_jay_pierrepont_moffat = { is_dead = no }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
		}
		NEE_john_winant = { remove_political_advisor_role = yes }
		hidden_effect = {
			NEE_jay_pierrepont_moffat = { set_nationality = ROOT }
			NEE_william_harriman = { set_character_flag = show_political_advisor_role }
		}
		activate_advisor = NEE_jay_pierrepont_moffat
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.461 option newengland.461.b"
		name = newengland.461.b #Harriman's our man!
		trigger = {
			NEE_william_harriman = {
				has_trait = NEE_ambassador_to_canada
				is_country_leader = no
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				has_government = social_liberal
			}
		}
		NEE_john_winant = { remove_political_advisor_role = yes }
		hidden_effect = {
			NEE_jay_pierrepont_moffat = { set_nationality = ROOT }
			NEE_william_harriman = { set_character_flag = show_political_advisor_role }
		}
		activate_advisor = NEE_william_harriman
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.461 option newengland.461.c"
		name = newengland.461.c #Demote the office
		add_political_power = 10
		NEE_john_winant = { remove_political_advisor_role = yes }
		hidden_effect = {
			NEE_jay_pierrepont_moffat = { set_nationality = ROOT }
			NEE_william_harriman = { set_character_flag = show_political_advisor_role }
		}
	}
}

					remove_political_advisor_role = yes

			}
		}
	}

## 500+ - Underground Railroad ##
# 500 - hidden LL
country_event = {
	id = newengland.500
	title = KR.hidden.t
	desc = KR.hidden.d

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag }
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.500 option 1"
		if = { #If downstream is closed, no missions
			limit = {
				261 = { has_state_flag = blocked_route } #Ohio
			}
			country_event = { id = newengland.500 days = 45 }
		}
		else_if = { #If Michigan is closed, furthest mission is Ohio
			limit = {
				393 = { has_state_flag = blocked_route } #Michigan
			}
			activate_mission = NEE_LL_Ohio_Albany_Route
		}
		else_if = { #If Minnesota is closed, furthest mission is Michigan
			limit = {
				391 = { has_state_flag = blocked_route } #Minnesota
			}
			activate_mission = NEE_LL_Michigan_Ohio_Route
		}
		else = { #Full Mission
			activate_mission = NEE_LL_Minnesota_Michigan_Route
		}
	}
}

# 505 - invite parallel group
state_event = {
	id = newengland.505
	title = newengland.505.t
	desc = newengland.505.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_refugees

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.505 option newengland.505.a"
		ai_chance = { base = 75 }
		name = newengland.505.a
		event_target:UR_state = { set_state_flag = helped_parallel_group }
		# Add partial patrol
		add_to_variable = { NEE.LL_people_route = 35 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:UR_state = { has_state_flag = completed_smuggle_group }
			}
			event_target:UR_state = { clr_state_flag = completed_smuggle_group }
			NEE = { NEE_LL_Success = yes }
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.505 option newengland.505.b"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				event_target:UR_state = {
					OR = {
						state = 261
						state = 359
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = newengland.505.b
		NEE = { NEE_LL_Success = yes }
	}
}

### 1940 elections ###
country_event = {
	id = newengland.600 #hidden event to fire the correct version of the election (donotlog)
	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = NEE_had_provisional_election
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = PSA_Leader
			has_country_flag = NEE_had_1940_election
		}
		has_democratic_government = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = newengland.209 days = 3 } # Reset the congress mechanic
		}
	}

	option = {
		set_country_flag = NEE_had_1940_election
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { character = NEE_lewis_barrows }
			}
			country_event = newengland.601 #Hurley vs Barrows
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { character = NEE_david_walsh }
			}
			country_event = newengland.602 #Walsh vs Winant
		}
		else = {
			country_event = newengland.603 #Hurley vs Winant
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Hurley vs Barrows
	id = newengland.601
	title = newengland.601.t
	desc = newengland.601.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NEE_Hurley_Barrows

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Democrat - Hurley
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.601 option newengland.601.a"
		name = newengland.601.a
		ai_chance = { base = 55 }
		promote_character = NEE_charles_hurley
		USA_progressive_democrats_elected_effect = yes
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = -0.03
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.03
		}
	}

	option = { # Republican - Barrows
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.601 option newengland.601.b"
		name = newengland.601.b
		ai_chance = { base = 75 }
		USA_republicans_elected_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			NEE_lewis_barrows = {
				remove_trait = { trait = NEE_provisional_president ideology = market_liberal_subtype }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			promote_character = NEE_charles_hurley
			country_event = { id = newengland.162 days = 635 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Walsh vs Winant
	id = newengland.602
	title = newengland.602.t
	desc = newengland.602.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NEE_Walsh_Winant

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Democrat - Walsh
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.602 option newengland.602.a"
		name = newengland.602.a
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		USA_progressive_democrats_elected_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			NEE_david_walsh = {
				remove_trait = { trait = NEE_provisional_president ideology = social_liberal_subtype }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			promote_character = NEE_john_winant
			country_event = { id = newengland.166 days = 305 }
			country_event = { id = newengland.219 days = 800 }
		}
	}

	option = { # Republican - Winant
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.602 option newengland.602.b"
		name = newengland.602.b
		ai_chance = { base = 60 }
		promote_character = NEE_john_winant
		USA_republicans_elected_effect = yes
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = -0.03
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = newengland.163 days = 176 }
			country_event = { id = newengland.164 days = 394 }
			country_event = { id = newengland.183 days = 1100 }
		}
	}
}

### 1944 elections ###
country_event = {
	id = newengland.604 #hidden event to fire the correct version of the election (donotlog)
	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = NEE_had_1940_election
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = PSA_Leader
			has_country_flag = NEE_had_1944_election
		}
		has_democratic_government = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = newengland.209 days = 3 } } # Reset the congress mechanic
	}

	option = {
		set_country_flag = NEE_had_1944_election
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { character = NEE_charles_hurley }
			}
			country_event = newengland.605 #Hurley vs Baldwin
		}
		else = {
			country_event = newengland.606 #Tobin vs Baldwin
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Hurley vs Baldwin
	id = newengland.605
	title = newengland.605.t
	desc = newengland.605.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NEE_Hurley_Baldwin

	is_triggered_only = yes

### 1948 elections ###
country_event = {
	id = newengland.607 #hidden event to fire the correct version of the election (donotlog)
	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = NEE_had_1944_election
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = PSA_Leader
			has_country_flag = NEE_had_1948_election
		}
		has_democratic_government = yes
	}

	option = {
		set_country_flag = NEE_had_1948_election
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { character = NEE_maurice_tobin }
			}
			country_event = newengland.608 #Tobin vs Aiken
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { character = NEE_raymond_baldwin }
			}
			country_event = newengland.609 #Harriman vs Baldwin
		}
		else = {
			country_event = newengland.610 #Harriman vs Aiken
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Tobin vs Aiken
	id = newengland.608
	title = newengland.608.t
	desc = newengland.608.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NEE_Tobin_Aiken

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Democrat - Tobin
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.608 option newengland.608.a"
		name = newengland.608.a
		USA_progressive_democrats_elected_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			promote_character = NEE_george_aiken
		}
	}

	option = { # Republican - Aiken
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event newengland.608 option newengland.608.b"
		name = newengland.608.b
		promote_character = NEE_george_aiken
		USA_republicans_elected_effect = yes
	}
}

### 1952 elections ###
country_event = {
	id = newengland.611 #hidden event to fire the correct version of the election (donotlog)
	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = NEE_had_1948_election
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = PSA_Leader
			has_country_flag = NEE_had_1952_election
		}
		has_democratic_government = yes
	}

	option = {
		set_country_flag = NEE_had_1952_election
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { character = NEE_george_aiken }
			}
			country_event = newengland.612 #Bowles vs Aiken
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { character = NEE_william_harriman }
			}
			country_event = newengland.613 #Harriman vs Dewey
		}
		else = {
			country_event = newengland.614 #Bowles vs Dewey
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = newengland.1000 #system event to add NEE's debuffs if they get the mainland after the ACW has ended (donotlog)
	hidden = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = CAN
			has_war_with = MEX
			country_exists = CSA
			country_exists = USA
			country_exists = TEX
			has_country_flag = already_got_acw_debuffs
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = { country_exists = PSA }
			is_in_faction_with = PSA
		}
	}

	option = {
		country_event = amcivwar.24
	}
}
